	    }
	    
	    function tcfAPIHandler() {
		var gdprApplies;

		    return queue;

function sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline () {
    if (sr_detect_operaMini || !("classList" in document.createElement("_"))) {
	return false;
    }
    var nav_trigger = document.getElementById('nav_trigger');
    if(!nav_trigger || nav_trigger.triggered) {
	return false;
    }
    nav_trigger.triggered = true;
    var nav = document.getElementById('nav');
    var nav_trigger_a = nav_trigger.querySelector('a');
    if (nav_trigger_a) {
	nav_trigger_a.setAttribute('href','javascript:void(0)');
	nav_trigger.onclick = function (event) {
	    nav.classList.toggle('open');
	    var is_open = nav.classList.contains('open');
	    if (is_open) {
		nav_trigger.classList.add('open');
	    }
	    else {
		nav_trigger.classList.remove('open');
	    }
	    event.preventDefault();
	    try { sr_record_analytics_event('MainNavButtonClick_inline',sr_record_directory(),sr_record_page());}
	    catch(err) {}
	};
    }
    return true;
}
sr_menus_setupMainNav_button_inline();

        <h4>The Most Powerful Research Tools in Sports.</h4>
        <p>Find any player, any team, any season, any game, any play.</p>
    </div>
    <p>
        <a href="https://stathead.com/?ref=bbr&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" class="button stathead_button" target="_blank"><strong>Subscribe Now</strong> (First Month Free)</a>
    </p>
</div>

<hr>

<div>
    <h4>Season and Career Finder</h4>
    Find single-season or multi-year totals to create leaderboards by team, height, age and more.
    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/dW9cQ?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Who is the leading left-handed shooting scorer in NBA history?</a>
    </div>
    <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/psl_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Player</a> &bull;
    <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/tsl_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Team</a>
</div>

<hr>

<div>
    <h4>Game Finder</h4>
    Find individual or groups of games matching a variety of criteria. Includes every game in NBA/BAA regular season and postseason history.
    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/8X7rP?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Who is the oldest player to score 30 points in a game?</a>
    </div>
    <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/pgl_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Player</a> &bull;
    <a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/tgl_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Team</a>
</div>

<hr>

<div>
    <h4><a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/quarter_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Player Quarter Finder</a></h4>
    Search for the best performances in a quarter by players in the digitized play-by-play era (since 1996-97).
    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/5A37h?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Who has the most 20-point quarters in a single season since 1996-97?</a>
    </div>
</div>

<hr>



<div>
    <h4><a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/pspan_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Player Span Finder</a></h4>
    Find the best/worst spans for any number of seasons, games or days. Find youngest/quickest players to statistical milestones.
    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/loEAL?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Which players have averaged 30+ PPG over a 5-season span?</a>
    </div>
</div>

<hr>

<div>
    <h4><a href="https://stathead.com/basketball/shot_finder.cgi?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Player Shot Finder</a></h4>
    Run customized searches through every NBA Field Goal Attempt in the digitized play-by-play era (since 1996-97).
    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/NgHy7?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Who has the most go-ahead shots in the final 24 seconds of the 4th quarter or overtime in a season since 1996-97?</a>
    </div>
</div>

    <div class="callout light">
        Ex: <a href="https://stathead.com/tiny/AW2P2?&utm_medium=bbr&utm_source=bbr_homepage&utm_campaign=basketball" target="_blank" rel='noopener'>Wilt Chamberlain vs Bill Russell</a>
